# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.33.0`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.33.0$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.33.0` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.33.0`

# Task: Implement Custom Header Injection Filter for Envoy

## Objective
Create a new HTTP filter `envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection` that injects
configurable headers into requests and/or responses based on route metadata.

## Requirements

1. **Create filter source files**:
   - `source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h` — filter class declaration
   - `source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.cc` — filter implementation
   - `source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.h` — factory declaration
   - `source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.cc` — factory registration

2. **Filter behavior**:
   - Implements `Http::StreamDecoderFilter` (request path) and `Http::StreamEncoderFilter` (response path)
   - Reads header injection rules from filter config
   - Supports both request and response header injection
   - Follows Envoy's filter lifecycle (decodeHeaders, encodeHeaders)

3. **Create test file**:
   - `test/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter_test.cc`

## Key Reference Files
- `source/extensions/filters/http/header_to_metadata/filter.h` — simple header filter pattern
- `source/extensions/filters/http/header_to_metadata/filter.cc` — implementation pattern
- `source/extensions/filters/http/header_to_metadata/config.cc` — factory registration
- `source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h` — factory base class

## Success Criteria
- Filter header file declares class inheriting from StreamDecoderFilter/StreamEncoderFilter
- Filter implementation has decodeHeaders/encodeHeaders methods
- Factory config file registers the filter
- Follows Envoy naming: envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection
- Test file exists

    13→    const envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::Config& config) {
    14→  for (const auto& rule : config.headers()) {
    15→    HeaderRule header_rule;
    16→    header_rule.header_name = rule.header_name();
    17→    header_rule.header_value = rule.header_value();

    21→  }
    22→}

    26→

    29→Http::FilterHeadersStatus CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::decodeHeaders(
    30→    Http::RequestHeaderMap& headers, bool) {

    33→  // Inject headers into request

    36→      headers.setReference(Http::LowerCaseString(rule.header_name), rule.header_value);
    37→    }
    38→  }
    39→
    40→  return Http::FilterHeadersStatus::Continue;

Perfect! I have successfully implemented the custom header injection filter for Envoy. Here's a summary of what has been created:

## Implementation Summary

### Files Created

**Filter Implementation (Source Code):**
1. **filter.h** - Filter class declaration
   - `Config` class that stores header rules from protobuf config
   - `CustomHeaderInjectionFilter` class implementing both `StreamDecoderFilter` and `StreamEncoderFilter`
   - Methods for request and response header injection

2. **filter.cc** - Filter implementation
   - `Config::Config()` - Parses header rules from protobuf config
   - `decodeHeaders()` - Injects headers matching `apply_to_request=true`
   - `encodeHeaders()` - Injects headers matching `apply_to_response=true`
   - Helper methods for callbacks

3. **config.h** - Factory configuration declaration
   - `CustomHeaderInjectionConfig` class inheriting from `FactoryBase`
   - Registered as "envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection"

4. **config.cc** - Factory implementation
   - `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()` - Creates filter instances
   - `createRouteSpecificFilterConfigTyped()` - Creates per-route configs
   - `REGISTER_FACTORY` macro for filter registration

**Tests:**
5. **filter_test.cc** - Comprehensive test suite
   - Tests request header injection
   - Tests response header injection
   - Tests headers applied to both paths
   - Tests empty configuration
   - Tests passthrough of data/trailers

**Configuration:**
6. **custom_header_injection.proto** - Protobuf schema
   - `Config` message with repeated `HeaderRule` entries
   - Each rule specifies header name, value, and whether to apply to request/response

7. **BUILD files** (2)
   - Source BUILD file defining libraries and extensions
   - Test BUILD file with test configuration

struct HeaderRule {
  std::string header_name;
  std::string header_value;
  bool apply_to_request;
  bool apply_to_response;

2. WRITE /workspace/source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.cc
#include "source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h"

#include "envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.pb.h"

#include "source/common/http/utility.h"

namespace Envoy {
namespace Extensions {
namespace HttpFilters {
namespace CustomHeaderInjectionFilter {

Config::Config(
    const envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::Config& config) {
  for (const auto& rule : config.headers()) {
    HeaderRule header_rule;
    header_rule.header_name = rule.header_name();
    header_rule.header_value = rule.header_value();
    header_rule.apply_to_request = rule.apply_to_request();
    header_rule.apply_to_response = rule.apply_to_response();
    header_rules_.emplace_back(header_rule);
  }
}

CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::CustomHeaderInjectionFilter(const ConfigSharedPtr config)
    : config_(config) {}

CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::~CustomHeaderInjectionFilter() = default;

Http::FilterHeadersStatus CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::decodeHeaders(
    Http::RequestHeaderMap& headers, bool) {
  const auto* config = getConfig();

  // Inject headers into request
  for (const auto& rule : config->headerRules()) {
    if (rule.apply_to_request) {
      headers.setReference(Http::LowerCaseString(rule.header_name), rule.header_value);
    }
  }

  return Http::FilterHeadersStatus::Continue;
}

void CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::setDecoderFilterCallbacks(
    Http::StreamDecoderFilterCallbacks& callbacks) {
  decoder_callbacks_ = &callbacks;
}

Http::FilterHeadersStatus CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::encodeHeaders(
    Http::ResponseHeaderMap& headers, bool) {
  const auto* config = getConfig();

  // Inject headers into response
  for (const auto& rule : config->headerRules()) {
    if (rule.apply_to_response
... (truncated)

4. WRITE /workspace/source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.cc
#include "source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.h"

#include <string>

#include "envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.pb.h"
#include "envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.pb.validate.h"
#include "envoy/registry/registry.h"

#include "source/common/protobuf/utility.h"
#include "source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h"

namespace Envoy {
namespace Extensions {
namespace HttpFilters {
namespace CustomHeaderInjectionFilter {

Http::FilterFactoryCb CustomHeaderInjectionConfig::createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped(
    const envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::Config& proto_config,
    const std::string&, Server::Configuration::FactoryContext&) {
  ConfigSharedPtr filter_config(std::make_shared<Config>(proto_config));

  return [filter_config](Http::FilterChainFactoryCallbacks& callbacks) -> void {
    callbacks.addStreamFilter(
        Http::StreamFilterSharedPtr{new CustomHeaderInjectionFilter(filter_config)});
  };
}

absl::StatusOr<Router::RouteSpecificFilterConfigConstSharedPtr>
CustomHeaderInjectionConfig::createRouteSpecificFilterConfigTyped(
    const envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::Config& config,
    Server::Configuration::ServerFactoryContext&, ProtobufMessage::ValidationVisitor&) {
  return std::make_shared<const Config>(config);
}

/**
 * Static registration for the custom header injection filter.
 */
REGISTER_FACTORY(CustomHeaderInjectionConfig, Server::Configuration::NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory);

} // namespace CustomHeaderInjectionFilter
} // namespace HttpFilters
} // namespace Extensions
} // namespace Envoy

6. WRITE /workspace/api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.proto
syntax = "proto3";

package envoy.extensions.filters.http.custom_header_injection.v3;

import "udpa/annotations/status.proto";
import "udpa/annotations/versioning.proto";
import "validate/validate.proto";

option java_package = "io.envoyproxy.envoy.extensions.filters.http.custom_header_injection.v3";
option java_outer_classname = "CustomHeaderInjectionProto";
option java_multiple_files = true;
option go_package = "github.com/envoyproxy/go-control-plane/envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3;custom_header_injectionv3";
option (udpa.annotations.file_status).package_version_status = ACTIVE;

// [#protodoc-title: Custom Header Injection Filter]
//
// The configuration for injecting custom headers into requests and/or responses.
//
// Custom Header Injection :ref:`configuration overview <config_http_filters_custom_header_injection>`.
// [#extension: envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection]

message Config {
  option (udpa.annotations.versioning).previous_message_type =
      "envoy.extensions.filters.http.custom_header_injection.v3.Config";

  // HeaderRule defines a header to inject.
  message HeaderRule {
    // The name of the header to inject.
    string header_name = 1 [(validate.rules).string = {
      well_known_regex: HTTP_HEADER_NAME
      strict: false
    }];

    // The value of the header to inject.
    string header_value = 2;

    // Whether to apply this header to request headers.
    bool apply_to_request = 3;

    // Whether to apply this header to response headers.
    bool apply_to_response = 4;
  }

  // The list of header rules to apply.
  repeated HeaderRule headers = 1;
}
